Abstract: Computing the conditional mode of a distribution, better known as the $\mathit{maximum\ a\ posteriori}$ (MAP) assignment, is a fundamental task in probabilistic inference. However, MAP estimation is generally intractable, and remains hard even under many common structural constraints and approximation schemes. We introduce $\mathit{probably\ approximately\ correct}$ (PAC) algorithms for MAP inference that provide provably optimal solutions under variable and fixed computational budgets. We characterize tractability conditions for PAC-MAP using information theoretic measures that can be estimated from finite samples. Our PAC-MAP solvers are efficiently implemented using probabilistic circuits with appropriate architectures. The randomization strategies we develop can be used either as standalone MAP inference techniques or to improve on popular heuristics, fortifying their solutions with rigorous guarantees. ### [165] [On the Intrinsic Dimensions of Data in Kernel Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.16139)
*Rustem Takhanov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了流形假设下核岭回归的泛化性能，提出了两种内在维度概念，分析了它们与Kolmogorov n-宽度的关系，并给出了误差界和估计算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流形假设认为当输入分布支撑的内在维度较低时，机器学习方法的泛化性能会显著提升。本文旨在研究核岭回归中内在维度的不同定义及其对泛化性能的影响。

Method: 提出了两种内在维度定义：基于核诱导度量的Minkowski维度d_ρ和基于Kolmogorov n-宽度衰减的有效维度d_K。分析了n-宽度与积分算子特征值的关系，证明了n-宽度刻画了所有概率测度下的最坏特征值衰减。提出了使用有限样本估计n-宽度上界的算法。

Result: 推导了约束核岭回归的过拟合误差界O(n^{-(2+d_K)/(2+2d_K)+ε})。证明了对于接近均匀的分布，使用O(ε^{-d_ρ}log(1/ε))样本可以高概率计算所有n-宽度的ε-准确上界。计算了各种分形集的有效维度d_K，发现对于拉普拉斯核等，d_K可以显著小于d_ρ。

Conclusion: 有效维度d_K比Minkowski维度d_ρ更能准确刻画核岭回归的泛化性能，特别是在不规则域上。提出的算法可以实用地估计内在维度，为理解核方法的泛化行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: The manifold hypothesis suggests that the generalization performance of machine learning methods improves significantly when the intrinsic dimension of the input distribution's support is low. In the context of KRR, we investigate two alternative notions of intrinsic dimension. The first, denoted $d_ρ$, is the upper Minkowski dimension defined with respect to the canonical metric induced by a kernel function $K$ on a domain $Ω$. The second, denoted $d_K$, is the effective dimension, derived from the decay rate of Kolmogorov $n$-widths associated with $K$ on $Ω$. Given a probability measure $μ$ on $Ω$, we analyze the relationship between these $n$-widths and eigenvalues of the integral operator $φ\to \int_ΩK(\cdot,x)φ(x)dμ(x)$. We show that, for a fixed domain $Ω$, the Kolmogorov $n$-widths characterize the worst-case eigenvalue decay across all probability measures $μ$ supported on $Ω$. These eigenvalues are central to understanding the generalization behavior of constrained KRR, enabling us to derive an excess error bound of order $O(n^{-\frac{2+d_K}{2+2d_K} + ε})$ for any $ε> 0$, when the training set size $n$ is large. We also propose an algorithm that estimates upper bounds on the $n$-widths using only a finite sample from $μ$. For distributions close to uniform, we prove that $ε$-accurate upper bounds on all $n$-widths can be computed with high probability using at most $O\left(ε^{-d_ρ}\log\frac{1}ε\right)$ samples, with fewer required for small $n$. Finally, we compute the effective dimension $d_K$ for various fractal sets and present additional numerical experiments. Our results show that, for kernels such as the Laplace kernel, the effective dimension $d_K$ can be significantly smaller than the Minkowski dimension $d_ρ$, even though $d_K = d_ρ$ provably holds on regular domains.

</details>


### [166] [Beat-ssl: Capturing Local ECG Morphology through Heartbeat-level Contrastive Learning with Soft Targets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.16147)
*Muhammad Ilham Rizqyawan,Peter Macfarlane,Stathis Hadjidemetriou,Fani Deligianni*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 获取标注的ECG数据用于监督学习模型具有挑战性。现有的对比学习框架要么只关注全局上下文，要么未能充分利用ECG特有的特征，且依赖硬对比目标，无法充分捕捉ECG信号中特征相似性的连续特性。

Method: 提出Beat-SSL对比学习框架，通过节律级和心跳级的双上下文对比学习，使用软目标来更好地捕捉ECG特征相似性的连续特性。在预训练后，将模型应用于两个下游任务：多标签分类（全局节律评估）和ECG分割。

Conclusion: Beat-SSL通过双上下文对比学习和软目标，有效解决了ECG数据标注困难的问题，在有限标注数据下实现了与大规模预训练基础模型相当甚至更好的性能，特别是在ECG分割任务中表现突出。

Abstract: Obtaining labelled ECG data for developing supervised models is challenging. Contrastive learning (CL) has emerged as a promising pretraining approach that enables effective transfer learning with limited labelled data. However, existing CL frameworks either focus solely on global context or fail to exploit ECG-specific characteristics. Furthermore, these methods rely on hard contrastive targets, which may not adequately capture the continuous nature of feature similarity in ECG signals. In this paper, we propose Beat-SSL, a contrastive learning framework that performs dual-context learning through both rhythm-level and heartbeat-level contrasting with soft targets. We evaluated our pretrained model on two downstream tasks: 1) multilabel classification for global rhythm assessment, and 2) ECG segmentation to assess its capacity to learn representations across both contexts. We conducted an ablation study and compared the best configuration with three other methods, including one ECG foundation model. Despite the foundation model's broader pretraining, Beat-SSL reached 93% of its performance in multilabel classification task and surpassed all other methods in the segmentation task by 4%.

### [167] [Learning to Discover at Test Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.16175)
*Mert Yuksekgonul,Daniel Koceja,Xinhao Li,Federico Bianchi,Jed McCaleb,Xiaolong Wang,Jan Kautz,Yejin Choi,James Zou,Carlos Guestrin,Yu Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TTT-Discover通过测试时强化学习让LLM针对特定问题持续训练，在多个科学领域实现了新的最先进成果，且使用开源模型和较低成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 如何利用AI发现科学问题的新最先进解决方案？现有测试时扩展方法（如AlphaEvolve）使用冻结的LLM进行搜索，而TTT-Discover通过在测试时进行强化学习，让LLM能够针对特定测试问题获得经验并持续训练。

Method: TTT-Discover采用测试时训练方法，通过强化学习让LLM针对特定问题持续学习。学习目标和搜索子程序专门设计为优先考虑最有希望的解决方案，这与传统持续学习不同，目标是产生一个优秀解决方案而非平均表现好的多个方案。

Result: 在数学、GPU内核工程、算法设计和生物学等多个领域的几乎所有尝试问题上都实现了新的最先进成果：包括Erdős最小重叠问题、自相关不等式、GPUMode内核竞赛（比先前技术快2倍）、AtCoder算法竞赛以及单细胞分析中的去噪问题。所有结果都使用开源模型OpenAI gpt-oss-120b实现，成本仅为每个问题几百美元。

Abstract: How can we use AI to discover a new state of the art for a scientific problem? Prior work in test-time scaling, such as AlphaEvolve, performs search by prompting a frozen LLM. We perform reinforcement learning at test time, so the LLM can continue to train, but now with experience specific to the test problem. This form of continual learning is quite special, because its goal is to produce one great solution rather than many good ones on average, and to solve this very problem rather than generalize to other problems. Therefore, our learning objective and search subroutine are designed to prioritize the most promising solutions. We call this method Test-Time Training to Discover (TTT-Discover). Following prior work, we focus on problems with continuous rewards. We report results for every problem we attempted, across mathematics, GPU kernel engineering, algorithm design, and biology. TTT-Discover sets the new state of the art in almost all of them: (i) Erdős' minimum overlap problem and an autocorrelation inequality; (ii) a GPUMode kernel competition (up to $2\times$ faster than prior art); (iii) past AtCoder algorithm competitions; and (iv) denoising problem in single-cell analysis. Our solutions are reviewed by experts or the organizers. All our results are achieved with an open model, OpenAI gpt-oss-120b, and can be reproduced with our publicly available code, in contrast to previous best results that required closed frontier models. Our test-time training runs are performed using Tinker, an API by Thinking Machines, with a cost of only a few hundred dollars per problem.

### [168] [Counterfactual Training: Teaching Models Plausible and Actionable Explanations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.16205)
*Patrick Altmeyer,Aleksander Buszydlik,Arie van Deursen,Cynthia C. S. Liem*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为"反事实训练"的新训练范式，利用反事实解释来增强模型的可解释性，使模型在训练阶段就学习生成合理且可操作的反事实解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反事实解释方法大多是后处理技术，虽然能生成合理且可操作的反事实解释，但模型本身并不具备这种解释能力。研究者希望让模型在训练阶段就直接学习生成高质量的反事实解释，而不是依赖后处理。

Method: 提出反事实训练方法，在训练阶段使用反事实解释来最小化学习到的表示与合理、可操作解释之间的差异。通过将反事实解释融入训练目标，使模型具备内在生成高质量反事实解释的能力。

Result: 实证和理论分析表明，该方法能够训练出具备内在生成理想反事实解释能力的模型，同时模型还表现出改进的对抗鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 反事实训练是一种有效的训练范式，能够使模型在保持性能的同时，具备更好的可解释性和鲁棒性，为构建更可信的决策系统提供了新思路。

Abstract: We propose a novel training regime termed counterfactual training that leverages counterfactual explanations to increase the explanatory capacity of models. Counterfactual explanations have emerged as a popular post-hoc explanation method for opaque machine learning models: they inform how factual inputs would need to change in order for a model to produce some desired output. To be useful in real-world decision-making systems, counterfactuals should be plausible with respect to the underlying data and actionable with respect to the feature mutability constraints. Much existing research has therefore focused on developing post-hoc methods to generate counterfactuals that meet these desiderata. In this work, we instead hold models directly accountable for the desired end goal: counterfactual training employs counterfactuals during the training phase to minimize the divergence between learned representations and plausible, actionable explanations. We demonstrate empirically and theoretically that our proposed method facilitates training models that deliver inherently desirable counterfactual explanations and additionally exhibit improved adversarial robustness.

</details>

### [169] [Verified polynomial-time reductions in Lean 4: formalizing the complexity of decision-relevant information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.15571)
*Tristan Simas*

Main category: cs.CC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个Lean 4框架，用于形式化多项式时间归约和复杂性理论证明，并应用该框架形式化分析了决策相关信息识别问题的复杂性，证明了该问题在显式和简洁编码下的多种复杂性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究决策问题中哪些坐标足以计算最优行动的复杂性（SUFFICIENCY-CHECK问题），旨在形式化验证复杂性理论中的结果，建立可验证的复杂性分析框架。

Method: 开发了Lean 4形式化框架，包含捆绑的Karp归约和多项式时间见证、组合引理/策略、以及NP/coNP和Σ₂ᴾ成员性和难解性模板。使用该框架形式化分析了SUFFICIENCY-CHECK问题的复杂性。

Result: 形式化验证了SUFFICIENCY-CHECK问题的复杂性：coNP完全性；来自SET-COVER的(1-ε)ln n不可近似性；在ETH下简洁编码的2^Ω(n)下界；自然参数化的W[2]-难解性；以及显式与简洁模型之间的二分性。

Conclusion: 成功构建了一个可扩展的Lean 4框架用于复杂性理论的形式化验证，并应用该框架获得了SUFFICIENCY-CHECK问题的全面复杂性特征，展示了形式化方法在复杂性理论中的可行性。

Abstract: We present a Lean 4 framework for polynomial-time reductions and complexity-theory proofs, and use it to formalize the complexity of identifying decision-relevant information. Problem: given a decision problem, which coordinates suffice to compute an optimal action? (SUFFICIENCY-CHECK; explicit encodings). Verified complexity results (Lean): coNP-complete; $(1-\varepsilon)\ln n$ inapproximable (from SET-COVER); $2^{Ω(n)}$ lower bounds under ETH for succinct encodings; W[2]-hard for a natural parameterization; and a dichotomy between explicit and succinct models. Formalization contributions: bundled Karp reductions with polynomial-time witnesses; composition lemmas/tactics; and templates for NP/coNP and $Σ_2^P$ membership and hardness. Scale: about 5,600 lines of Lean across 36 files, with 230+ theorems and explicit polynomial bounds.

</details>


### [170] [DNF formulas are efficiently testable with relative error](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.16076)
*Xi Chen,William Pires,Toniann Pitassi,Rocco A. Servedio*

Main category: cs.CC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个多项式查询算法，用于在相对误差模型中测试任意未知布尔函数是否为s项DNF公式，这是首个在相对误差模型中具有常数查询复杂度的丰富自然函数类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对误差模型是布尔函数性质测试中一个具有挑战性的框架，最近在多个工作中被引入和研究。目前缺乏能够处理依赖超常数数量变量的丰富自然函数类的高效测试算法。

Method: 提出了一种新颖的分解方法，将任意s项DNF公式分解为"局部簇"的项。这种分解使得算法能够在DNF公式未明确给出的情况下有效利用结构信息。

Result: 开发了一个poly(s,1/ε)查询算法，用于测试任意未知函数是否为s项DNF公式，这是首个在相对误差模型中具有常数查询复杂度的丰富自然函数类。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了新的DNF分解方法在算法设计中的有效性，即使在DNF未明确给出的情况下也能应用，这种分解方法可能在其他上下文中也有应用价值。

Abstract: We give a poly$(s,1/ε)$-query algorithm for testing whether an unknown and arbitrary function $f: \{0,1\}^n \to \{0,1\}$ is an $s$-term DNF, in the challenging relative-error framework for Boolean function property testing that was recently introduced and studied in a number of works [CDH+25b, CPPS25a, CPPS25b, CDH+25a]. This gives the first example of a rich and natural class of functions which may depend on a super-constant number of variables and yet is efficiently testable in the relative-error model with constant query complexity.
  A crucial new ingredient enabling our approach is a novel decomposition of any $s$-term DNF formula into ``local clusters'' of terms. Our results demonstrate that this new decomposition can be usefully exploited for algorithms even when the $s$-term DNF is not explicitly given; we believe that this decomposition may have applications in other contexts.

</details>

### [171] [Existential Positive Transductions of Sparse Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.15890)
*Nikolas Mählmann,Sebastian Siebertz*

Main category: cs.DM

TL;DR: 该论文研究了单子稳定图类的稀疏化猜想，提出了存在正稀疏化猜想，并验证了其在已知特例中的正确性，同时引入了新的组合操作"subflip"来刻画无共匹配的单子稳定类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单子稳定性概括了结构图论中的许多"驯服"概念，如平面性、有界度、有界树宽和无处稠密性。稀疏化猜想预测，单子稳定图类可以通过一阶转换从无处稠密类中逻辑编码。本文旨在研究更受限的存在正稀疏化猜想，探索无共匹配的单子稳定类是否可以通过仅使用存在正一阶公式从无处稠密类中转换得到。

Method: 1. 引入新的组合操作"subflip"，作为flip操作在无共匹配情况下的自然类比；2. 使用subflip操作，通过加强已知的flip-flatness和flipper游戏特征来刻画无共匹配的单子稳定性片段；3. 验证存在正稀疏化猜想在所有已知特例中的正确性；4. 探索将结果推广到更强大的MSO逻辑。

Result: 1. 验证了存在正稀疏化猜想在所有已知的原始猜想特例中成立；2. 发现稀疏原像可以作为稠密输入图的子图找到；3. 成功刻画了无共匹配的单子稳定性片段；4. 发现(重新发现)在关系结构上，(存在)正MSO逻辑与(存在)正FO逻辑具有相同的表达能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出了存在正稀疏化猜想并验证了其在已知特例中的正确性，引入了subflip操作作为研究无共匹配单子稳定性的关键工具，同时揭示了在关系结构上正MSO逻辑并不比正FO逻辑更强大，为单子稳定性的稀疏化研究提供了新的视角和方法。

Abstract: Monadic stability generalizes many tameness notions from structural graph theory such as planarity, bounded degree, bounded tree-width, and nowhere density. The sparsification conjecture predicts that the (possibly dense) monadically stable graph classes are exactly those that can be logically encoded by first-order (FO) transductions in the (always sparse) nowhere dense classes. So far this conjecture has been verified for several special cases, such as for classes of bounded shrub-depth, and for the monadically stable fragments of bounded (linear) clique-width, twin-width, and merge-width.
  In this work we propose the existential positive sparsification conjecture, predicting that the more restricted co-matching-free, monadically stable classes are exactly those that can be transduced from nowhere dense classes using only existential positive FO formulas. While the general conjecture remains open, we verify its truth for all known special cases of the original conjecture. Even stronger, we find the sparse preimages as subgraphs of the dense input graphs.
  As a key ingredient, we introduce a new combinatorial operation, called subflip, that arises as the natural co-matching-free analog of the flip operation, which is a central tool in the characterization of monadic stability. Using subflips, we characterize the co-matching-free fragment of monadic stability by appropriate strengthenings of the known flip-flatness and flipper game characterizations for monadic stability. In an attempt to generalize our results to the more expressive MSO logic, we discover (rediscover?) that on relational structures (existential) positive MSO has the same expressive power as (existential) positive FO.

</details>


### [172] [Characterizations of monadically dependent tree-ordered weakly sparse structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.16039)
*Hector Buffière,Yuquan Lin,Jaroslav Nešetřil,Patrice Ossona de Mendez,Sebastian Siebertz*

Main category: cs.DM

TL;DR: 该论文研究了树序弱稀疏结构的单调依赖性，通过多种构造方法（如Gaifman图变体、诱导/非诱导树序子式等）给出了单调依赖性的特征刻画，并建立了与稀疏理论的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 树序弱稀疏结构在描述有界灌木深度、有界结构扩张、有界团宽度等图类时常用作树模型。研究这类结构的单调依赖性有助于理解这些重要图类的逻辑性质。

Method: 论文考虑了树序结构的多种构造方法：树序Gaifman图变体、树序关联图、诱导和非诱导树序子式、广义基本图等。通过这些构造方法对树序弱稀疏结构类进行特征刻画。

Result: 建立了树序弱稀疏结构类单调依赖性的多个特征刻画，证明了这类结构单调依赖当且仅当其稀疏化是无处稠密的。同时将团宽度和线性团宽度的有界性转化为树宽度和路径宽度的有界性。

Conclusion: 论文为树序弱稀疏结构类提供了单调依赖性的完整理论框架，建立了与稀疏理论的桥梁，并首次给出了排除子式的图类的模型论特征刻画，为结构图论开辟了新视角。

Abstract: A class of structures is monadically dependent if one cannot interpret all graphs in colored expansions from the class using a fixed first-order formula. A tree-ordered $σ$-structure is the expansion of a $σ$-structure with a tree-order. A tree-ordered $σ$-structure is weakly sparse if the Gaifman graph of its $σ$-reduct excludes some biclique (of a given fixed size) as a subgraph. Tree-ordered weakly sparse graphs are commonly used as tree-models (for example for classes with bounded shrubdepth, structurally bounded expansion, bounded cliquewidth, or bounded twin-width), motivating their study on their own. In this paper, we consider several constructions on tree-ordered structures, such as tree-ordered variants of the Gaifman graph and of the incidence graph, induced and non-induced tree-ordered minors, and generalized fundamental graphs.
  We provide characterizations of monadically dependent classes of tree-ordered weakly sparse $σ$-structures based on each of these constructions, some of them establishing unexpected bridges with sparsity theory. As an application, we prove that a class of tree-ordered weakly sparse structures is monadically dependent if and only if its sparsification is nowhere-dense. Moreover, the sparsification transduction translates boundedness of clique-width and linear clique-width into boundedness of tree-width and path-width. We also prove that first-order model checking is not fixed parameter tractable on independent hereditary classes of tree-ordered weakly sparse graphs (assuming $AW[*]\neq FPT$) and give what we believe is the first model-theoretical characterization of classes of graphs excluding a minor, thus opening a new perspective of structural graph theory.

</details>


### [173] [All ascents exponential from valued constraint graphs of pathwidth three](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.16156)
*Artem Kaznatcheev,Willemijn Volgering*

Main category: cs.DM

TL;DR: 本文研究了组合优化问题中的严格局部搜索算法，发现即使是在路径宽度为3的简单值约束图上，所有严格局部搜索算法都可能被迫采取指数级步数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究组合优化问题中伪布尔函数的严格局部搜索算法复杂性，探索值约束满足问题（VCSP）的约束图稀疏性如何影响算法性能，特别是路径宽度作为自然稀疏参数的重要性。

Method: 通过分析值约束满足问题的约束图特性，提出路径宽度作为关键稀疏参数。构建了"受控加倍构造"：一个路径宽度为3的值约束满足问题，其中从指定初始赋值开始的所有上升路径都是指数级长度。

Result: 改进了先前研究：之前构建的稀疏VCSP中所有上升路径为指数长度的实例路径宽度≥4，而本文构造的实例路径宽度仅为3。证明即使在路径宽度为3的简单值约束图上，所有严格局部搜索算法都可能需要指数级步数。

Conclusion: 路径宽度是理解严格局部搜索算法能力限制的自然稀疏参数。即使在路径宽度为3的简单值约束图上，所有严格局部搜索算法都可能被迫采取指数级步数，这为组合优化问题的算法设计提供了重要理论边界。

Abstract: Many combinatorial optimization problems can be formulated as finding as assignment that maximized some pseudo-Boolean function (that we call the fitness function). Strict local search starts with some assignment and follows some update rule to proceed to an adjacent assignment of strictly higher fitness. This means that strict local search algorithms follow ascents in the fitness landscape of the pseudo-Boolean function. The complexity of the pseudo-Boolean function (and the fitness landscapes that it represents) can be parameterized by properties of the valued constraint satisfaction problem (VCSP) that encodes the pseudo-Boolean function. We focus on properties of the constraint graphs of the VCSP, with the intuition that spare graphs are less complex than dense ones. Specifically, we argue that pathwidth is the natural sparsity parameter for understanding limits on the power of strict local search. We show that prior constructions of sparse VCSPs where all ascents are exponentially long had pathwidth greater than or equal to four. We improve this this with our controlled doubling construction: a valued constraint satisfaction problem of pathwidth three where all ascents are exponentially long from a designated initial assignment. From this, we conclude that all strict local search algorithms can be forced to take an exponential number of steps even on simple valued constraint graphs of pathwidth three.

</details>
